              <h3 class="video-title">
               Suspect in Craigslist missing couple case turns self in
              </h3>
              <div class="datestamp">
               <span data-trans="Published">

            <div class="video-fulltitle" style="display: none;">
             Suspect in Craigslist missing couple case turns self in
            </div>
            <div class="video-fulldescription">
             <h3>
              Suspect in Craigslist missing couple case turns self in
             </h3>
             <ul class="font_color">
              <li>
               <span data-trans="published:">
                published:
               </span>
               <span class="strong">
                26 Jan 2015
               </span>
              </li>
              <li>
               <span data-trans="views:">
                views:
               </span>
               <span class="strong">
                8
               </span>
              </li>
             </ul>
             <p>
              ATLANTA (AP)  Authorities say the man who last had phone contact with a Georgia couple who went missing after driving across the state to check out a classic car sought in a Craigslist ad has turned himself in on charges related to the case.

Investigators had obtained warrants for 28-year-old Ronnie Adrian Jay Towns on charges of giving false statements and criminal attempt to commit theft by deception. Authorities said Towns was taken into custody Monday morning.

He hasnt been accused of harming 69-year-old Elrey Bud Runion and his wife, 66-year-old June Runion.

The Runions are from Marietta, outside Atlanta. On Thursday, they drove to McRae, three hours south, to meet someone who responded to Buds online ad seeking a 1966 Mustang.

Telfair County Sheriff Chris Steverson tells WMAZ-TV in Macon Towns was interviewed, and information he provided didnt match what investigators already knew.

To read the original story, go here....
             </p>

          <div class="wikiparser">
           <h3>
            Craigslist
           </h3>
           <div class="mwcss wikisnippet">
            <div class="mediawiki ltr sitedir-ltr ns-0 skin-vector">
             <div class="mwp">
              <img height="31" src="http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Craigslist.svg/120px-Craigslist.svg.png" style="float:right; padding: 0 0 10px 10px" width="120"/>
              <p>
               <b>
                Craigslist
               </b>
               is a
               <a href="http://wn.com/Classified_advertising" title="Classified advertising">
                classified advertisements
               </a>
               website with sections devoted to jobs, housing,
               <a href="http://wn.com/Personal_advertisement" title="Personal advertisement">
                personals
               </a>
               , for sale, services,
               <a href="http://wn.com/Community_service" title="Community service">
                community
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="http://wn.com/Gig_(musical_performance)" title="Gig (musical performance)">
                gigs
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="http://wn.com/R%C3%A9sum%C3%A9" title="Rsum">
                rsums
               </a>
               , and discussion forums.
              </p>
              <p>
               <a href="http://wn.com/Craig_Newmark" title="Craig Newmark">
                Craig Newmark
               </a>
               began the service in 1995 as an email distribution list of friends, featuring local events in the
               <a href="http://wn.com/San_Francisco_Bay_Area" title="San Francisco Bay Area">
                San Francisco Bay Area
               </a>
               , before becoming a web-based service in 1996 and expanding into other classified categories. It started expanding to other U.S. cities in 2000, and currently covers 50 countries.
              </p>
              <p>
               Having observed people helping one another in friendly, social, and trusting communal ways on the Internet via the
               <a class="mw-redirect" href="http://wn.com/WELL_(virtual_community)" title="WELL (virtual community)">
                WELL
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="http://wn.com/MindVox" title="MindVox">
                MindVox
               </a>
               and
               <a href="http://wn.com/Usenet" title="Usenet">
                Usenet
               </a>
               , and feeling isolated as a relative newcomer to San Francisco, Craigslist founder
               <a href="http://wn.com/Craig_Newmark" title="Craig Newmark">
                Craig Newmark
               </a>
               decided to create something similar for local events. In early 1995, he began an email distribution list to friends. Most of the early postings were submitted by Newmark and were notices of social events of interest to software and Internet developers living and working in the
               <a href="http://wn.com/San_Francisco_Bay_Area" title="San Francisco Bay Area">
                San Francisco Bay Area
               </a>
               .
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="wikipage">
            <span class="btn btn-primary" data-trans="Read more..." onclick="return load_wiki(this, 'Craigslist', 1)" style="margin-top: 20px;">
             Read more...
            </span>
           </div>
           <br/>
           <br/>

             http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Craigslist

  <script>
   function defineAspectRatio() {

            jQuery('.image-frame img').each(function(index) {

                jQuery(this).css('width', '100%');
                jQuery(this).css('height', 'auto');

                var parentWidth = jQuery(this).parent('.image-frame').width();
                var parentHeight = jQuery(this).parent('.image-frame').height();
                var imgWidth = jQuery(this).width();
                var imgHeight = jQuery(this).height();

                    if(imgWidth == imgHeight) {
                        jQuery(this).addClass('squa');

                        jQuery('#tracker').append('|' + imgWidth + '&amp;' + parentWidth + '|');

                        if(parentHeight &lt; parentWidth) {
                            jQuery(this).css('width', '100%');
                            jQuery(this).css('height', 'auto');
                        } else if(parentHeight &gt; parentWidth) {
                            jQuery(this).css('height', '100%');
                            jQuery(this).css('width', 'auto');
                        }

                    } else if(imgWidth &lt; imgHeight) {
                        jQuery(this).addClass('port');
                        jQuery(this).css('width', '100%');
                    } else if(imgWidth &gt; imgHeight) {
                        jQuery(this).addClass('land');
                        jQuery(this).css('height', '100%');
                    }

                });

imageShimmy();

};

function imageShimmy() {

    jQuery('.image-frame img').each(function(index) {

        var parentWidth_sp = jQuery(this).parent('.image-frame').width();
        var parentHeight_sp = jQuery(this).parent('.image-frame').height();
        var imgWidth_sp = jQuery(this).width();
        var imgHeight_sp = jQuery(this).height();

        var imgWidthShimmy = (imgWidth_sp - parentWidth_sp)/2;
        var imgHeightShimmy = (imgHeight_sp - parentHeight_sp)/2;

                    if(jQuery(this).hasClass('land') &amp;&amp; imgWidth_sp &lt; parentWidth_sp) {
                        jQuery(this).css('width', '100%');
                        jQuery(this).css('height', 'auto');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin', '0');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin-top', '-' + imgHeightShimmy + 'px');
                    } else if(jQuery(this).hasClass('land') &amp;&amp; imgWidth_sp &gt; parentWidth_sp) {
                        jQuery(this).css('margin-left', '-' + imgWidthShimmy + 'px');
                    } else if(jQuery(this).hasClass('port') &amp;&amp; imgHeight_sp &lt; parentHeight_sp) {
                        jQuery(this).css('height', '100%');
                        jQuery(this).css('width', 'auto');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin', '0');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin-left', '-' + imgWidthShimmy + 'px');
                    } else if(jQuery(this).hasClass('port') &amp;&amp; imgHeight_sp &gt; parentHeight_sp) {
                        jQuery(this).css('margin-top', '-' + imgHeightShimmy + 'px');
                    } else if(jQuery(this).hasClass('squa') &amp;&amp; imgHeight_sp &lt; parentHeight_sp) {
                        jQuery(this).css('height', '100%');
                        jQuery(this).css('width', 'auto');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin', '0');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin-top', '-' + imgHeightShimmy + 'px');
                    } else if(jQuery(this).hasClass('squa') &amp;&amp; imgHeight_sp &gt; parentHeight_sp) {
                        jQuery(this).css('width', '100%');
                        jQuery(this).css('height', 'auto');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin', '0');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin-top', '-' + imgHeightShimmy + 'px');
                    } else if(jQuery(this).hasClass('squa') &amp;&amp; imgWidth_sp &lt; parentWidth_sp) {
                        jQuery(this).css('height', '100%');
                        jQuery(this).css('width', 'auto');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin', '0');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin-left', '-' + imgWidthShimmy + 'px');
                    } else if(jQuery(this).hasClass('squa') &amp;&amp; imgWidth_sp &gt; parentWidth_sp) {
                        jQuery(this).css('height', '100%');
                        jQuery(this).css('width', 'auto');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin', '0');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin-left', '-' + imgWidthShimmy + 'px');
                    };

                    jQuery(this).animate({
                        opacity: 1},
                        200, function() {
                        // stuff to do after animation is complete
                    });


                });
}



jQuery(window).load(function() {

    defineAspectRatio();

});
  </script>

    $(function(){
				var playerPosition = $('#playercontainer1').offset();

		        $(".search-type a").click(function () {
		
		            var search_type = $(this).data('type');		
		            $("#search-selector").val(search_type);
		                if(!$(this).hasClass("active"))
		                {
		                    $(".search-type a").removeClass("active");		
		                    $(this).addClass("active");		
		                }
		        });
		        $('#mainsearch').submit(function(event) {
		            var search_type = $("#search-selector").val();					
		            if(search_type == 'videos') {
		                var search_string = $(".top_query").val();
		                search_string = search_string.toLowerCase().replace(/[\.\/\: _!]+/g, '_');
		                window.open('http://wn.com/' + search_string, '_blank');
		                return false; // do not submit the form
		            }else{
		                return true;
		            }
		         });
				 
				$(".gotop").live("click", function(){
					$('html, body').animate({scrollTop: playerPosition.top}, "slow");
				});

				$(".logo-bm li").live("click", function(){
  					$(".logo-bm li").removeClass("active");
  					$(this).addClass("active")
				});
				$('.local_news').click(function () {
					loadLocalNews();
			   	});
				$( ".nav li" ).click(function() {
				     if ( $( this ).hasClass( "local" ) ) {
						$('#page-title').hide();
						$('#article-links').hide();
				    }else{
						$('#page-title').show();
						$('#article-links').show();
					}
				});

            // switch to the Videos tab and start playing the first video
            jQuery('#main-image-link').on('click', function(e) {
                jQuery('ul#left-nav &gt; li &gt; a.videos').fadeOut('slow').fadeIn('slow');
                jQuery('ul#left-nav &gt; li &gt; a.videos').click();
                // a somewhat aproximate way of playing the default playlist under the "Videos" left menu link
                window.videoplayers[1].playVideo();
            });

            // focus on the email field when a user clicks the subscribe btn
            jQuery('#dLabel').on('click', function(e) {
                jQuery('#subscribe-email').focus();
            });
            jQuery('.emailTool').tooltip();


		});
        // --&gt;
  </script>
  <script language="JavaScript">
   &lt;!--
    // overwriting geoip methods for backwards compatibility
    var weather_data;
    var available_langs = {};
    var country_code;

    function get_ip_data_and_focus(callback) {
        $.getJSON( "http://ip-api.com/json/?callback=", function(data) {
            weather_data = data;
            country_code = geoip_country_code();
			var country_code = data.countryCode;
				var country_code = country_code.toLowerCase();
				var country = data.country;
				var geo_obj = $('.weather-wdgt');
				var city = data.city;
				var user_country = data.country;
				var lat = data.lat;
				var lng = data.lon;
				$('.user-country').html(country);
				if (city.length &gt; 1) {
					$('.user-city').prepend(city).show();
				}
				$('.flag').addClass('flag-'+country_code);
				var sel = $('#country option').filter(function(index) {
						return ($(this).text() == country)
				});

		// look for languages alternatives using our geonaming service
		function showCountrySelection(geocode_data) {
			jQuery.ajax({
                url: '/api/upge/cheetah-photo-search/geoname',
                data: {country: geocode_data.countryCode, style: 'full'},
                dataType: 'jsonp',
                type: 'GET',
                success: function(data, status) {
                    if (data.geonames) {
                        var geonamelangs = data.geonames[0].languages
                        langs = geonamelangs.split(',')
                        if (langs.length == 0) {
                        	return false;
                        }
                        // only pick the first language
                        first_lang = langs[0]
						if (window.available_langs[first_lang] == undefined) {
							$('#language option').filter(function () {
						   return ($(this).text() == 'English');
							}).attr('selected','selected');
						}
						var lang = window.available_langs[first_lang].langname;

						$('#language option').filter(function () {
						   return ($(this).text() == lang);
							}).attr('selected','selected');

                    }
                }
            });
		}



    get_ip_data_and_focus();

    var geoip_city = function() {
        if (weather_data == undefined) {
            return '';
        }
        return weather_data.city;
    };
    var geoip_country_name = function() {
        if (weather_data == undefined) {
            return '';
        }
        return weather_data.country;
    };
    var geoip_country_code = function() {
        if (weather_data == undefined) {
            return '';
        }
        return weather_data.countryCode;
    };
    var geoip_latitude = function() {
        if (weather_data == undefined) {
            return '';
        }
        return weather_data.lat;
    };
    var geoip_longitude = function() {
        if (weather_data == undefined) {
            return '';
        }
        return weather_data.lon;
    };
	function get_weather_data(geo_obj, lat, lng, country_code){
		  first_geo_data = true;
		  var global_geo_obj = geo_obj;
		  jQuery.ajax({
		      data: {
		          lat: jQuery.trim(lat),
		          lng: jQuery.trim(lng),
		          cnt: 1,
		      },
		      dataType: 'jsonp',
		      url: 'http://article.wn.com/api/upge/cheetah-photo-search/weather_findcity',
		      success: function(data) {
		          //weather_data = data.list[0];  ;
		          weather_info = ''
		          for (idx in data.list) {
		              weather_data = data.list[idx]
		              if (weather_data) {
		                weather = weather_data.weather[0]
				  		tempC = parseInt(parseFloat(weather_data.main.temp)-273.15)
				 		tempF = parseInt(tempC*1.8+32)
						weather_info += '&lt;img src="http://cdn0.wn.com/or/images/weather/95/'+weather.icon+'.png" alt="" class="pull-left" /&gt;'
						if (country_code == 'us'){
							weather_info += '&lt;p class="pull-left"&gt;'+tempF+'&lt;/p&gt;&lt;span class="pull-left letter"&gt;F&lt;/span&gt;'
						}else{
							weather_info += '&lt;p class="pull-left"&gt;'+tempC+'&lt;/p&gt;&lt;span class="fa fa-circle-o pull-left"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="pull-left letter"&gt;C&lt;/span&gt;'
						}
		             }
		          }
		          global_geo_obj.html(weather_info);
		      },
		  });
		};
		function loadLocalNews(country) {
			if(! country){
				var country = $("#country").val().toLowerCase();
			};
			var language = $("#language").val().toLowerCase();
            var sub = (language=='english'?'edition/'+country:'local/'+language)
            document.location = 'http://wn.com/#/'+sub;
        }
		function load_wiki(el, query, main) {
	        var wikisnippet = jQuery(el).closest('.wikiparser').find('.wikisnippet');
	        jQuery(el).html('Loading... please wait...');
	        jQuery(el).closest('div').load('/api/upge/cheetah-photo-search/wiki_page?main='+main+'&amp;query='+escape(query), function(){
	            wikisnippet.hide();
	        });
	        return false;
	    }
